<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нестерпимый.html>нестерпи́мый</a> (9573)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стерпеть.html>стерпе́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sterpétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́мый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ímyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нестерпимый.html>нестерпи́мый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nesterpímyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>unbearable</li></ol>

***нести.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нести.html>нести́</a> (871)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*nestì</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нести.html>нести́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nestí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понести.html>понести́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bear, to bring, to carry
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нести.html>нести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тяжелый.html>тяжёлые</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сумка.html>су́мки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nestí</b> tjažólyje súmki</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>to carry</b> heavy bags</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to carry, to bear, to support
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>они́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:должный.html>должны́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нести.html>нести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ответственность.html>отве́тственность</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ошибка.html>оши́бки</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oní dolžný <b>nestí</b> otvétstvennostʹ za ošíbki.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">They need <b>to bear</b> responsibility for the mistakes.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to lay (eggs)
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снести.html>снести́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">snestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to talk (about), to babble on (about)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вздор.html>вздор</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нести.html>несёт</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">što (za vzdor) on <b>nesjót</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">what (utter) nonsense he is talking!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>понима́ю</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:там.html>там</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нести.html>несёт</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne ponimáju, što oná tam <b>nesjót</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">I have no idea what she is babbling on about</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be carried away, to go over the limits
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1931</b>,  Ильф <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> Петров (Ilf and Petrov),  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ru:%D0%97%D0%BE%D0%BB%D0%BE%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%B9_%D1%82%D0%B5%D0%BB%D1%91%D0%BD%D0%BE%D0%BA" class="extiw" title="w:ru:Золотой телёнок"><a href = vnd.unilang:золотой.html>Золото́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:теленок.html>телёнок</a></a></cite>  | <cite>The Little Golden Calf</cite> | :</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">— росси́я <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вас</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:забыть.html>забу́дет</a>! — <a href = vnd.unilang:рявкнуть.html>ря́вкнул</a> Остап. Ипполит Матвеевич, <a href = vnd.unilang:держать.html>держа́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>руке́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сладкий.html>сла́дкий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пирожок.html>пирожо́к</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:недоумение.html>недоуме́нием</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слушать.html>слу́шал</a> Остапа, <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:удержать.html>удержа́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нельзя.html>нельзя́</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нести.html>несло́</a></b>. <a href = vnd.unilang:великий.html>Вели́кий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:комбинатор.html>комбина́тор</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чувствовать.html>чу́вствовал</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вдохновение.html>вдохнове́ние</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:упоительный.html>упои́тельное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:состояние.html>состоя́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a> вышесредним <a href = vnd.unilang:шантаж.html>шантажо́м</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пройтись.html>прошёлся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:комната.html>ко́мнате</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:барс.html>барс</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">— Rossíja vas ne zabúdet! — rjávknul Ostap. Ippolit Matvejevič, deržá v ruké sládkij pirožók, s nedouménijem slúšal Ostapa, no uderžátʹ jevó býlo nelʹzjá. Jevó <b>nesló</b>. Velikij kombinátor čúvstvoval vdoxnovénije, upoítelʹnoje sostojánije pered vyšesrednim šantažóm. On prošelsja po kómnate, kak bars.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">"Russia will never forget you!" bellowed Ostap. Ippolit Matveyevich, holding a sweet bun in his hand, listened to Ostap in perplexity but was unable to hold him. He was <b>carried away</b>. The great combinator felt inspiration, ravishing condition before the upper-middle class blackmailing.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1931</b>,  Ильф <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> Петров (Ilf and Petrov),  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ru:%D0%97%D0%BE%D0%BB%D0%BE%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%B9_%D1%82%D0%B5%D0%BB%D1%91%D0%BD%D0%BE%D0%BA" class="extiw" title="w:ru:Золотой телёнок"><a href = vnd.unilang:золотой.html>Золото́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:теленок.html>телёнок</a></a></cite>  | <cite>The Little Golden Calf</cite> | :</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">Остап <a href = vnd.unilang:отогнать.html>отогна́л</a> Полесова <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> Никеши <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> Влади <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:неподдельный.html>неподде́льной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:суровость.html>суро́востью</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:спросить.html>спроси́л</a>:<br /> — <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:какой.html>како́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:полок.html>полку́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:служить.html>служи́ли</a>? <a href = vnd.unilang:прийтись.html>Придётся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:послужить.html>послужи́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отечество.html>оте́честву</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>Вы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дворянин.html>дворя́не</a>? <a href = vnd.unilang:очень.html>О́чень</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хороший.html>хорошо́</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:запад.html>за́пад</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>нам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:помочь.html>помо́жет</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:крепиться.html>крепи́тесь</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:полный.html>по́лная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тайна.html>та́йна</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вклад.html>вкла́дов</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:организация.html>организа́ции</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:внимание.html>внима́ние</a>. <br />Остапа <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нести.html>несло́</a></b>. <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>Дело</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:будто.html>бу́дто</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:налаживаться.html>нала́живалось</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ostap otognál Polesova ot Nikeši i Vladi i s nepoddélʹnoj suróvostʹju sprosíl:<br /> — V kakóm polku služíli? Pridetsja poslužítʹ otéčestvu. Vy dvorjáne? Očenʹ xorošó. Západ nam pomóžet. Krepítesʹ. Pólnaja tájna vkládov, to jestʹ organizácii. Vnimánije. <br />Ostapa <b>nesló</b>. Delo kak búdto naláživalosʹ.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Ostap drove Polesov away from Mikesha and Vladya and asked with genuine harshness: "In which regiment did you serve? You'll have to serve your motherland. Are you noblemen? Very well. The West is going to help us. Hold on. Full secrecy of accounts, I mean, organization. Attention." Ostap got <b>carried away</b>. The business seemed to go smoothly.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нести.html>Нести́</a></b> and <a href = vnd.unilang:понести.html>понести́</a> are concrete verbs. Their counterpart, <a href = vnd.unilang:носить.html>носи́ть</a>, is an abstract verb.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_2">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="derivedterms" style="column-count: 2; -moz-column-count: 2; -ms-column-count: 2; -o-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2;;">

***нестись.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нестись.html>нести́сь</a> (2977)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нести.html>нести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-сь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нестись.html>нести́сь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nestísʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пронестись.html>пронести́сь</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:донестись.html>донести́сь</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">снести́сь</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hurtle, to dash, to race, to tear, to scurry <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to move rapidly, violently, or without control</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to come, <i>(sound)</i> to reach one's ears, to be heard
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:окно.html>окна́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нестись.html>несётся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:запах.html>за́пах</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гарь.html>га́ри</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">iz okná <b>nesjótsja</b> zápax gári</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">there's the smell of burning coming from the window</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to lay eggs
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">снести́сь</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">snestísʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нести.html>нести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нестись.html>нести́сь</a></b> is a concrete verb. The counterpart, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:носиться.html>носи́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nosítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, is an abstract verb.
</p>

***несуразный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:несуразный.html>несура́зный</a> (21351)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">not</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">сура́зный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">suráznyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">prominent, beautiful</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">су-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">su-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">with</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>раз</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">(originally) stroke, cut</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несуразный.html>несура́зный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nesuráznyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> absurd, ridiculous</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> awkward, unsteady</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:несчастливый.html>несчастли́вый</a> (16536)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:счастливый.html>счастли́вый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sčastlívyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несчастливый.html>несчастли́вый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nesčastlívyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>unfortunate, ill-fated, ill-starred, luckless
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:несчастливый.html>несчастли́вый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>день</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nesčastlívyj</b> denʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">unlucky day</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***нет.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a> (59)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">нѣту</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nětu</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*nětu</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ne</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">not</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*e</i>, short form of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*estь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">is</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*tu</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">there, here</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">net</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>no
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:еще.html>ещё</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ješčó <b>net</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">not yet</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">net</span>) (<i>impersonal verb</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>there is no, there are no (+ <i>genitive</i>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:здесь.html>Здесь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́г</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Zdesʹ <b>net</b> doróg.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">There are no roads here.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́г</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U menjá <b>net</b> knig.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I have no books. (literally, “There are no books with me.”)</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Jevó <b>net</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He’s not here. (literally, “There is no him [here].”)</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The past tense of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">net</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">né bylo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and the future tense is <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бу́дет</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne búdet</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***нету.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>не́ту</a> (1693)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">нѣту</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nětu</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">нѣтъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nětŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. From older <b>*<a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> ѥ <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>ту</a></b> (it is not here), where <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>ту</a></b> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тут.html>тут</a>, also colloquial <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">не́туть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nétutĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), was originally an ethical dative (<i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">-ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-tĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, dative <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">-ти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Predicative">Predicative</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>не́ту</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nétu</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">proscribed<span class="ib-comma">,</span> low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> there is no, there are no (+ <i>genitive</i>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изменение.html>измене́ний</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>не́ту</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Izmenénij <b>nétu</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">There are no changes.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:карандаш.html>карандаше́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>не́ту</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U menjá karandašéj <b>nétu</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I have no pencils.</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">There are no pencils with me.</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Often proscribed in favor of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">net</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li>
<li>In the colloquial register, usage depends largely on the speaker's personal attitude towards this word; there is a range from active users to those who oppose it unconditionally.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">net</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>
<ol><li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="разговорное">разг.</span>-<span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="сниженное">сниж.</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:иметься.html>име́ется</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:отсутствовать.html>отсу́тствует</a> <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">[Григорий]: <a href = vnd.unilang:хозяйка.html>Хозя́йка</a>! <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:изба.html>избе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>друго́го</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:угол.html>угла́</a>? [<a href = vnd.unilang:хозяйка.html>Хозя́йка</a>]: <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>Не́ту</a></span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:родить.html>роди́мый</a>. </span></li>
</ul></li>


<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="устаревшее">устар.</span>, <span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> знач. <a href = vnd.unilang:частица.html>части́цы</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a> (<i><a href = vnd.unilang:отрицательный.html>отрица́тельный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ответ.html>отве́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вопрос.html>вопро́с</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:выражение.html>выраже́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несогласие.html>несогла́сия</a></i>) <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:неубедительный.html>неубеди́тельный</a> (16549)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:убедительный.html>убеди́тельный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ubedítelʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:неуверенность.html>неуве́ренность</a> (10349)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неуверенный.html>неуве́ренный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">neuvérennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>

***неугодный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:неугодный.html>неуго́дный</a> (23046)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:угодный.html>уго́дный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ugódnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неугодный.html>неуго́дный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neugódnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>disliked <i>(by)</i>, out of favour <i>(with)</i></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">угомон(и́ть)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ugomon(ítʹ)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неугомонный.html>неугомо́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neugomónnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> restless
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:неугомонный.html>неугомо́нный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребёнок</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>neugomónnyj</b> rebjónok</i> ― <span class="e-translation">fidgety child</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> indefatigable, ever-active</li></ol>
